\DoxyCodeLine{2798                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (charCode == 9)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2800                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} tabSize = m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.TabWidth * currentElementScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2801                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} tabs = Mathf.Ceil(m\_xAdvance / tabSize) * tabSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2802                     m\_xAdvance = tabs > m\_xAdvance ? tabs : m\_xAdvance + tabSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2803                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2804                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_monoSpacing != 0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2807 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3471                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.MatchAspect:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472                                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} yDelta = (1 -\/ ((characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x + characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x) / characterInfos[i].aspectRatio)) / 2; \textcolor{comment}{// Center of Rectangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3474                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = yDelta + (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x / characterInfos[i].aspectRatio); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = yDelta + (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x / characterInfos[i].aspectRatio); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                            \#if TMP\_PROFILE\_ON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481                             Profiler.EndSample();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                            \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                            \#endregion End UV Mapping Options}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3489 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                            \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490                             xScale = characterInfos[i].scale * (1 -\/ m\_charWidthAdjDelta);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3493                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (canvasRenderMode)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494                             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RenderMode.ScreenSpaceOverlay:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496                                     xScale *= lossyScale / canvasScaleFactor;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RenderMode.ScreenSpaceCamera:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499                                     xScale *= isCameraAssigned ? lossyScale : 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RenderMode.WorldSpace:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502                                     xScale *= lossyScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3514                             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y0 = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
